  //<![CDATA[
    function loadScript(url, callback) {
      var script = document.createElement("script");
      script.type = "text/javascript";
    
      if (script.readyState) {  //Internet Explorer
          script.onreadystatechange = function() {
            if (script.readyState == "loaded" ||
                    script.readyState == "complete") {
              script.onreadystatechange = null;
              callback();
            }
          };
      } else {  //Other browsers
        script.onload = function() {
          callback();
        };
      }
    
      script.src = url;
      document.getElementsByTagName("head")[0].appendChild(script);
    }
    
    function initAppleId() {
      AppleID.auth.init({
        clientId : 'com.goodreads.app', 
        scope : 'name email',
        redirectURI: 'https://www.goodreads.com/apple_users/sign_in_with_apple_web',
        state: 'apple_oauth_state_ead625ff-7063-4e1d-bbaa-002e784bcecd'
      });
    }

<span id="freeTextContainer17104941236511716202">When twenty year old, professional witch hunter, Victor Steep is summoned to handle a case; he travels to the town of Beth's Hollow to find residing in the vast woods surrounding the town, a witch with a deadly obsession.<br/><br/>In the woods, Victor meets a mysterious and beautiful young lady named Clearly, and her kind, but cursed brother Fabian. Promising Clearly that he will lo</span>
  <span id="freeText17104941236511716202" style="display:none">When twenty year old, professional witch hunter, Victor Steep is summoned to handle a case; he travels to the town of Beth's Hollow to find residing in the vast woods surrounding the town, a witch with a deadly obsession.<br /><br />In the woods, Victor meets a mysterious and beautiful young lady named Clearly, and her kind, but cursed brother Fabian. Promising Clearly that he will look for a cure for her brother, Victor soon questions if he can keep that promise, for killing the malicious witch he was hired to hunt, became more complicated than expected. In Order to defeat the witch, Victor now must find a book that has been missing for nearly twenty years, or risk the fate of Clearly, Fabian, and the entire town of Beth's Hollow. Not to mention, if he should fail, losing the possession of his very own skull to the witch’s disturbing collection.</span>

<div id="review_889647487" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/889647487" />
    <a title="Taylor Bunker" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/26571360-taylor-bunker"><img alt="Taylor Bunker" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1435766972p2/26571360.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/889647487?book_show_action=true">Mar 23, 2014</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Taylor Bunker" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Taylor Bunker" href="/user/show/26571360-taylor-bunker">Taylor Bunker</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span> (Review from the author)


        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer889647487" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer5532897194296701891">Witch In The Woods, being my first book, I admit that I probably love it a little too much. I originally wrote it for creative writing class in 2009, and it literally took me four years to turn it into a book.<br/><br/>I didn't want Witch In The Woods to be like other Y.A. novels. I wanted it to be different, and I really think I succeeded with that goal.<br/><br/>When I finished writing it, I really missed the characters. I had been working with them for such a long time, and I didn't like the thought that it was </span>
  <span id="freeText5532897194296701891" style="display:none">Witch In The Woods, being my first book, I admit that I probably love it a little too much. I originally wrote it for creative writing class in 2009, and it literally took me four years to turn it into a book.<br /><br />I didn't want Witch In The Woods to be like other Y.A. novels. I wanted it to be different, and I really think I succeeded with that goal.<br /><br />When I finished writing it, I really missed the characters. I had been working with them for such a long time, and I didn't like the thought that it was over, which is why it's exciting that I am turning Witch In The Woods into a trilogy!<br /><br />Witch In The Woods is my baby, and though it is not perfect, I hope others will enjoy it as much as I do.</span>
  <a data-text-id="5532897194296701891" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

  <div class="left bodycol">

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Stacey" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Stacey" href="/user/show/29802858-stacey">Stacey</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/29802858-stacey?shelf=my-favorites">my-favorites</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/29802858-stacey?shelf=ya">ya</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/29802858-stacey?shelf=paramormal">paramormal</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/29802858-stacey?shelf=ya-fantasy">ya-fantasy</a>,

          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer886262481" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer17304205686794831428">I very much enjoyed Witch in the Woods. The story never lagged and the characters were fun and believable. It has a creepy but fun plot that keeps the reader wanting more and is spookily suspenseful with a few laugh out loud moments. I highly recomend Witch in the Woods, not only to teens and young adults,but to anyone who enjoys curling up on the couch with a warm blanket and a great spooky story.</span>

          </span>
        </div>

If you like books about witches this is a good one, you wont regret it.</span>

<div id="review_1199381619" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1199381619" />
    <a title="K.S. Marsden" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/16729923-k-s-marsden"><img alt="K.S. Marsden" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1420402689p2/16729923.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1199381619?book_show_action=true">Feb 13, 2015</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="K.S. Marsden" class="user" itemprop="url" name="K.S. Marsden" href="/user/show/16729923-k-s-marsden">K.S. Marsden</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1199381619" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer8759571217478238870">The year is 1601 and Victor Steep is a professional witch-hunter amidst the witch craze era. But he hunts the real dangers. And one such danger takes him to Beth's Hollow, where a witch in the woods has been terrifying the residents for generations.<br/><br/>This book has been on my reading list for ages, ever since it was featured on Keeley's Days of Indie last Christmas. (<a href='http://thenorthernwitchbooks.blogspot.co.uk/2014/12/indie-booktubers.html' rel='nofollow noopener'>Quick link to all the videos</a>)<br/>I did delay a bit, because I was worried that a) I might find it too similar to my work; or b) it would </span>
  <span id="freeText8759571217478238870" style="display:none">The year is 1601 and Victor Steep is a professional witch-hunter amidst the witch craze era. But he hunts the real dangers. And one such danger takes him to Beth's Hollow, where a witch in the woods has been terrifying the residents for generations.<br /><br />This book has been on my reading list for ages, ever since it was featured on Keeley's Days of Indie last Christmas. (<a href="http://thenorthernwitchbooks.blogspot.co.uk/2014/12/indie-booktubers.html" rel="nofollow noopener">Quick link to all the videos</a>)<br />I did delay a bit, because I was worried that a) I might find it too similar to my work; or b) it would disappoint.<br />And then I made the mistake of watching the film Into The Woods, and that just plain scarred me from anything Witch and Wood related for months!<br />Anyway, back on track - a) this book is an amazing and original story; b) see point a.<br /><br />This is set in the beginning of the 17th Century, when the witch craze affects Europe, and millions of innocent people die because of the ignorance and greed of their fellow man. This is touched upon in the book, acknowledging that this is happening; but Witch in the Woods focusses on Victor's story.<br />Victor hunts <i>real</i> witches. Because they exist, they are evil creatures that torment nearby towns and tear families apart. And they are not easy to kill.<br />Victor's deceased father also hunted witches, and despite a somewhat distant relationship between the two, Victor learnt everything from him. Which includes inheriting his beliefs that all witches (and their demons) are evil and must be killed.<br /><br />But everything is not as black and white as it seems, when Victor meets Clearly and her brother Fabian.<br /><br />The story has an modest feel, and you can believe it's set in 1601. There is drama, and intrigue, the tension suitably builds to the final fight.<br /><br />The characters are all strong.<br />Victor gets to discover more about his mother, who died when he was born. And he also gets to completely relearn everything he thought he knew about his father. With the letters, diary entries and memories, his father is a very tangible character.<br />Then of course you have the bad guy - a 400 year old with with an obsession for collecting skulls? I loved her. She was definitely my favourite character, the way she was playing with Victor, haunting his thoughts.<br /><br />So overall, a story I was completely swept along by, and a series I can't wait to continue!</span>
  <a data-text-id="8759571217478238870" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<div id="review_1034843202" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1034843202" />
    <a title="John Winston" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/16673620-john-winston"><img alt="John Winston" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1467070596p2/16673620.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1034843202?book_show_action=true">Aug 23, 2014</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="John Winston" class="user" itemprop="url" name="John Winston" href="/user/show/16673620-john-winston">John Winston</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1034843202" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer5723778895293178858">Not Your Everyday Paranormal<br/>	<br/>I was pleasantly pleased and surprised by Witch In The Woods. I love the title: simple yet elegant. Taylor Ann Bunker has an imagination out of this world and does her homework as well in this romping witch hunt set in colonial times. Victor Steep is the courageous witch hunter and hero who, against all odds, does battle against the, more than match, lethal witch. A good amount of chapters start with Steep reading from his journal which is a wonderful touch. <br/><br/>Bunker i</span>
  <span id="freeText5723778895293178858" style="display:none">Not Your Everyday Paranormal<br />	<br />I was pleasantly pleased and surprised by Witch In The Woods. I love the title: simple yet elegant. Taylor Ann Bunker has an imagination out of this world and does her homework as well in this romping witch hunt set in colonial times. Victor Steep is the courageous witch hunter and hero who, against all odds, does battle against the, more than match, lethal witch. A good amount of chapters start with Steep reading from his journal which is a wonderful touch. <br /><br />Bunker is masterful in the way she seamlessly weaves colorful descriptions and vivid details into the narrative, action, and dialog of the story. At times I felt like I was watching a movie. And if your heart wasn’t beating fast enough with fear in the dark woods of Beth’s Hollow, then it’ll beat for that YA young love when Steep runs into Clearly Willow. Bunker has a gift when it come to creating characters. I especially like the contrast between the characters: the true mark of a talented author. This is most evident in the dialog between Gammer and Steep. <br /><br />I read WITW in a day. This one has it all. The Misercorde Dagger is cool, but I gotta get me one of those dagger pistols and start a collection. <br /></span>
  <a data-text-id="5723778895293178858" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<span id="freeTextContainer1208491867049454253">4/5 That was awesome!!   <span id="freeText1208491867049454253" style="display:none">4/5 That was awesome!! Can't wait to get the next two and find out what happens with Clearly &amp; Fabian!<br /><br /><br /><br />Victor is a witch hunter that has been drafted to Beth's Hollow to determine who this witch is that has been harassing the townspeople for years. After more and more people reportedly go missing once they enter the woods, Victor takes the task upon himself to bring this witch down. Little did he know that he would begin to develop feelings for those he would meet in the woods or that he would develop a new found respect for his deceased father in the process. <br /><br />A solid 4/5, Witch in the Woods was a really fun start to another witch trilogy that I can't wait to continue! A debut novel from this author, you can tell how much she enjoyed writing the characters as the storyline progressed. Victor is one of my favorite characters that I read in 2014. I need to get books 2 and 3 ASAP!</span>

  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/2128102928" />
    <a title="Kristi Basic" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/39312004-kristi-basic"><img alt="Kristi Basic" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1421615546p2/39312004.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/2128102928?book_show_action=true">Oct 18, 2017</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Kristi Basic" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Kristi Basic" href="/user/show/39312004-kristi-basic">Kristi Basic</a>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="did not like it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">did not like it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer2128102928" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer12557450892510296682">I kept thinking it was going to get better... that the characters would actually have some meat to them at some point, but it just never happened. The little tidbits of character development that WERE there seemed like they were just shoved into the book in random areas where they didn't even fit. Character motivations were strange and robotic. <br/>There was no build up to the end scene... everything felt like it was being spoken to you in the world's most monotone voice. <br/>Will not be reading more. </span>

          </span>
        </div>

  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1214934085" />
    <a title="Carla" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/29544590-carla"><img alt="Carla" src="https://s.gr-assets.com/assets/nophoto/user/f_50x66-6a03a5c12233c941481992b82eea8d23.png" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1214934085" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer17598913123217899439">I chose to read this book based on the reviews on here but was put off shortly after starting it by grammatical and spelling errors. I thought perhaps this was because I was reading it on my kindle and there was a problem in the translation so I persevered. However, these continued (wrong uses of to and too etc.)and changes of tense in the same sentence and I had to give up reading it after a few chapters. It felt like it had been written by a child, and hadn't been proof read properly. Sorry, I</span>
  <span id="freeText17598913123217899439" style="display:none">I chose to read this book based on the reviews on here but was put off shortly after starting it by grammatical and spelling errors. I thought perhaps this was because I was reading it on my kindle and there was a problem in the translation so I persevered. However, these continued (wrong uses of to and too etc.)and changes of tense in the same sentence and I had to give up reading it after a few chapters. It felt like it had been written by a child, and hadn't been proof read properly. Sorry, I realise lots of readers loved it but it wasn't for me.</span>

  function submitShelfLink(unique_id, book_id, shelf_id, shelf_name, submit_form, exclusive) {
    var checkbox_id = 'shelf_name_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    var element = document.getElementById(checkbox_id)

    var checked = element.checked
    if (checked && exclusive) {
      // can't uncheck a radio by clicking it!
      return
    }
    if(document.getElementById("savingMessage")){
      Element.show('savingMessage')
    }
    var element_id = 'shelfInDropdownName_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    Element.update(element_id, "saving...");
    if (submit_form) {
      Element.hide('shelfDropdown_' + unique_id)
      var form = document.getElementById('addBookForm' + book_id)
      if (form) {
        form.shelf.value = shelf_name
        form.onsubmit()
      }
    }
    else {
      var action = checked ? 'remove' : ''
      element.checked = !element.checked
      new Ajax.Request('/shelf/add_to_shelf', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name)}, parameters:'book_id=' + book_id + '&name=' + shelf_name + '&a=' + action + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('YFJifN9GwQUQ1QaeZsL1ckZigKJkueCR6HiD8KG5tFnirW9P6HelmXLoMYnSVbuek8H7amOBjnE9AtMpFGPoXA==')})
    }
  }

  function shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name) {
    Element.update('shelfListfalse_' + book_id, request.responseText)
    afterShelfSave(checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name.escapeHTML())
  }

  function refreshGroupBox(group_id, book_id) {
    new Ajax.Updater('addGroupBooks' + book_id + '', '/group/add_book_box', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){refreshGroupBoxComplete(request, book_id);}, parameters:'id=' + group_id + '&book_id=' + book_id + '&refresh=true' + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('WYEerhg9BB7izrM2J07F2TbnwQAkGjLJQiFT0n9jXjbbfhOdLwxggoDzhCGT2Ys140S6yCMiXCmXWwMLyrkCMw==')})
  }

  <span id="freeText6144121165493951225" style="display:none">T. A. Bunker is the author and illustrator of the exciting YA Paranormal trilogy: ‘Witch In The Woods’.           $$('div.prototip').each(function(i){i.setStyle({zIndex: 6000})});
        }
      });

      newTip['wrapper'].addClassName('prototipAllowOverflow');

        $('bookCover_23464246').observe('prototip:shown', function () {
          $$('div.prototip').each(function (e) {
            if ($('bookCover_23464246').hasClassName('ignored')) {
              e.setStyle({'display': 'none'});
              return;
            }
            e.setStyle({'overflow': 'visible'});
          });
        });
      $('bookCover_23464246').observe('prototip:hidden', function () {
        $$('span.elementTwo').each(function (e) {
          if (e.getStyle('display') !== 'none') {
            var lessLink = e.next();
            swapContent(lessLink);
          }
        });
      });

//]]>
</script>

</li>
</ul>
</div>
